        function openRemSearch() { 
            var overlay = document.getElementById('rem-search-overlay');
            if(overlay) overlay.style.display = 'flex'; 
            var input = document.getElementById('rem-search-input');
            if(input) input.focus(); 
        }
        function closeRemSearch() { 
            var overlay = document.getElementById('rem-search-overlay');
            if(overlay) overlay.style.display = 'none'; 
        }

    <script type="5224f36ee0823bdc69f8703d-text/javascript">
    (function() {
        let cur = 0; const slides = document.querySelectorAll(".rem-slide-v3");
        const bar = document.getElementById("rem-bar");
        const duration = 6000; let start = Date.now();
        if(slides.length < 2) return;
        function updateSlider() {
            let elapsed = Date.now() - start;
            let progress = (elapsed / duration) * 100;
            if (progress >= 100) {
                progress = 0; start = Date.now();
                slides[cur].classList.remove("active");
                cur = (cur + 1) % slides.length;
                slides[cur].classList.add("active");
            }
            if(bar) bar.style.width = progress + "%";
            requestAnimationFrame(updateSlider);
        }
        updateSlider();
    })();
    </script>

<script type="5224f36ee0823bdc69f8703d-text/javascript">
/**
 * SISTEMA DE PERFORMANCE SUPREMO V5000 - PORTAL REMADOR
 * Foco: Adiar Scripts Pesados + Zero Bloqueio de Renderização
 */
(function () {
    "use strict";
    // Não carrega para editores ou admin para não bugar o Elementor
    if (document.body.classList.contains('elementor-editor-active') || document.body.classList.contains('wp-admin')) return;

    var scriptsLoaded = false;

    var loadEliteScripts = function() {
        if (scriptsLoaded) return;
        scriptsLoaded = true;

        // 1. CARREGAMENTO ADIADO DE ANÚNCIOS (ADSENSE)
        const ads = [
            'https://pagead2.googlesyndication.com/pagead/js/adsbygoogle.js?client=ca-pub-6158073538788256',
            'https://fundingchoicesmessages.google.com/i/pub-6158073538788256?ers=1'
        ];
        ads.forEach(src => {
            let s = document.createElement('script');
            s.src = src; s.async = true; s.setAttribute('crossorigin', 'anonymous');
            document.head.appendChild(s);
        });

        // 2. MONITORAMENTO DE NOVOS POSTS (Apenas se necessário)
        // Diminuímos a carga para o servidor: verifica a cada 2 minutos em vez de 1
        setTimeout(function() {
            var lastPostID = 0;
            var apiUrl = 'https://remador.com.br/wp-json/wp/v2/posts?per_page=1';
            
            function checkForNewPosts() {
                fetch(apiUrl).then(response => response.json()).then(data => {
                    if (data.length > 0) {
                        if (lastPostID === 0) { lastPostID = data[0].id; return; }
                        if (data[0].id > lastPostID) {
                            lastPostID = data[0].id;
                            if (typeof exibirAvisoNovoPost === "function") {
                                exibirAvisoNovoPost(data[0].title.rendered, data[0].link);
                            }
                        }
                    }
                }).catch(err => {});
            }
            setInterval(checkForNewPosts, 120000); 
        }, 3000);

        // 3. SWIPER (Carrega apenas se houver um carrossel na tela)
        if (document.querySelector('.swiper')) {
            let sw = document.createElement('script');
            sw.src = 'https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/npm/swiper@10/swiper-bundle.min.js';
            sw.defer = true; document.body.appendChild(sw);
        }
    };

    // GATILHOS DE ATIVAÇÃO: Interação do usuário ou 5 segundos de espera
    window.addEventListener('scroll', loadEliteScripts, {once: true, passive: true});
    window.addEventListener('touchstart', loadEliteScripts, {once: true, passive: true});
    window.addEventListener('mousemove', loadEliteScripts, {once: true, passive: true});
    setTimeout(loadEliteScripts, 5000);

    // 4. POPUP DE URGÊNCIA (Simples e sem travas)
    window.addEventListener('scroll', function() {
        var popup = document.getElementById('rem-popup-urgente');
        if (popup && !popup.classList.contains('rem-popup-visible')) {
            var scrollPercent = (window.scrollY / (document.documentElement.scrollHeight - window.innerHeight)) * 100;
            if (scrollPercent > 45) popup.classList.add('rem-popup-visible');
        }
    }, {passive: true});
})();
</script>        <script type="5224f36ee0823bdc69f8703d-text/javascript">
        // Simple click handler for all blur images
        document.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
            if (e.target.tagName === 'IMG' && e.target.getAttribute('data-omni-mobile-blur') === 'true') {
                const fullSrc = e.target.getAttribute('data-omni-full-src');
                
                if (fullSrc) {
                    e.target.src = fullSrc;
                    e.target.style.filter = 'none';
                    e.target.classList.add('omni-full-loaded');
                }
                
                e.preventDefault();
                e.stopPropagation();
            }
        });
        
        // Handle overlay clicks
        document.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
            if (e.target.classList.contains('omni-blur-overlay') || e.target.classList.contains('omni-blur-text')) {
                const container = e.target.closest('.omni-blur-container');
                const img = container ? container.querySelector('img[data-omni-mobile-blur="true"]') : null;
                
                if (img) {
                    const fullSrc = img.getAttribute('data-omni-full-src');
                    
                    if (fullSrc) {
                        img.src = fullSrc;
                        img.style.filter = 'none';
                        img.classList.add('omni-full-loaded');
                        e.target.style.display = 'none';
                    }
                }
                
                e.preventDefault();
                e.stopPropagation();
            }
        });

        // Handle image load events to ensure descriptions stay visible
        document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
            // Process all blur images on page load
            const blurImages = document.querySelectorAll('img.omni-mobile-blur');
            blurImages.forEach(function(img) {
                // Check if we're on mobile
                const isMobile = window.innerWidth <= 768 || 
                    /Android|webOS|iPhone|iPad|iPod|BlackBerry|IEMobile|Opera Mini/i.test(navigator.userAgent);
                
                // If desktop, load full image immediately
                if (!isMobile && img.getAttribute('data-omni-full-src')) {
                    img.src = img.getAttribute('data-omni-full-src');
                    img.style.filter = 'none';
                    img.classList.add('omni-full-loaded');
                }
            });
        });

				const lazyloadRunObserver = () => {
					const lazyloadBackgrounds = document.querySelectorAll( `.e-con.e-parent:not(.e-lazyloaded)` );
					const lazyloadBackgroundObserver = new IntersectionObserver( ( entries ) => {
						entries.forEach( ( entry ) => {
							if ( entry.isIntersecting ) {
								let lazyloadBackground = entry.target;
								if( lazyloadBackground ) {
									lazyloadBackground.classList.add( 'e-lazyloaded' );
								}
								lazyloadBackgroundObserver.unobserve( entry.target );
							}
						});
					}, { rootMargin: '200px 0px 200px 0px' } );
					lazyloadBackgrounds.forEach( ( lazyloadBackground ) => {
						lazyloadBackgroundObserver.observe( lazyloadBackground );
					} );
				};
				const events = [
					'DOMContentLoaded',
					'elementor/lazyload/observe',
				];
				events.forEach( ( event ) => {
					document.addEventListener( event, lazyloadRunObserver );
				} );
			</script>

		<script id="spc-lazy-js" type="5224f36ee0823bdc69f8703d-text/javascript">
			(function () {
			const timeout = setTimeout(loadDelayed, 10000);
			const userEvents = ["mouseover", "keydown", "touchstart", "touchmove", "wheel"];

			function triggerLoad() {
				loadDelayed();
				clearTimeout(timeout);
				userEvents.forEach(e => {
				window.removeEventListener(e, triggerLoad)
				});
			}

			function loadDelayed() {
				document.querySelectorAll("script[data-spc-src]").forEach(el => {
				el.src = el.dataset.spcSrc
				});
			}

			userEvents.forEach(e =>
				window.addEventListener(e, triggerLoad, {passive: true})
			);
			}());
		</script>
		<script type="5224f36ee0823bdc69f8703d-text/javascript">
document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded",function(){
    const sticky = document.querySelector(".rem-nav-sticky-box");
    const placeholder = document.getElementById("rem-sticky-placeholder");
    if(!sticky || !placeholder) return;

    let stickyOffset, stickyHeight;
    let isFixed = false;
    let ticking = false;

    function updateMeasurements(){
        const wasFixed = isFixed;
        if(wasFixed) {
            sticky.classList.remove("rem-is-fixed");
            placeholder.style.height = "0px";
        }
        stickyOffset = placeholder.offsetTop;
        stickyHeight = sticky.offsetHeight;
        if(wasFixed) {
            sticky.classList.add("rem-is-fixed");
            placeholder.style.height = stickyHeight + "px";
        }
    }

    function update(){
        const shouldFix = window.scrollY >= stickyOffset;
        if(shouldFix !== isFixed){
            placeholder.style.height = shouldFix ? stickyHeight + "px" : "0px";
            sticky.classList.toggle("rem-is-fixed", shouldFix);
            isFixed = shouldFix;
        }
        ticking = false;
    }

    updateMeasurements();

    window.addEventListener("scroll", function(){
        if(!ticking){
            window.requestAnimationFrame(update);
            ticking = true;
        }
    }, {passive:true});

    window.addEventListener("resize", updateMeasurements);
});
</script>
    <script type="5224f36ee0823bdc69f8703d-text/javascript">

    (function() {

        // 1. Corrige Nomes dos Botões de Compartilhar

        const shareButtonsBlue = document.querySelectorAll('.rem-share-icon-blue');

        const shareButtonsWhite = document.querySelectorAll('.rem-share-icon-white');

        const shareBtnV10 = document.querySelectorAll('.rem-btn-share-v10');



        shareButtonsBlue.forEach(btn => btn.setAttribute('aria-label', 'Compartilhar notícia no WhatsApp'));

        shareButtonsWhite.forEach(btn => btn.setAttribute('aria-label', 'Compartilhar notícia'));

        shareBtnV10.forEach(btn => btn.setAttribute('aria-label', 'Abrir opções de compartilhamento'));



        // 2. Corrige Atributo ALT das Imagens (SEO e Acessibilidade)

        const googleNewsImg = document.querySelector('img[data-src*="Google_News_icon"]');

        if(googleNewsImg) googleNewsImg.setAttribute('alt', 'Siga o Remador no Google News');



        const adsImg = document.querySelector('div.jl_ads_wrap_sec img');

        if(adsImg) adsImg.setAttribute('alt', 'Publicidade do Remador');

        

        // 3. Corrige o Contraste do Menu "Últimas" via JS para garantir

        const menuUltimas = document.querySelector('a[href*="ultimas-noticias"]');

        if(menuUltimas) menuUltimas.style.color = "#d30c0c"; 

    })();

    </script>

        function acceptRemPrivacy() {
            localStorage.setItem('rem_privacy_accepted', 'true');
            const bar = document.getElementById('rem-privacy-bar');
            bar.style.opacity = '0';
            bar.style.transition = '0.3s';
            setTimeout(() => { bar.style.display = 'none'; }, 300);
        }
        document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", function() {
            if (!localStorage.getItem('rem_privacy_accepted')) {
                setTimeout(() => { 
                    const bar = document.getElementById('rem-privacy-bar');
                    if(bar) bar.style.display = 'block'; 
                }, 2000);
            }
        });
        </script>
